﻿﻿ Pakistan  ke Wazeer e Azam  Nawaz  shareef naay ansdadِ polio ke aalmi din ke mauqa par malik se is marz ke jald khatmay ka azm zahir karte hue kaha hai ke is maqsad ke liye malik mein polio emergency nafiz ki gayi hai
Pakistan  duniya mein polio se sab se ziyada mutasirah malik hai aur rawan baras yahan polio ke do so se ziyada naye mareez samnay aa chuke hain jo ke aik naya record hai
Wazeer e Azam  house se jari honay walay bayan ke mutabiq jummey ko polio ki rokkk thaam ke aalmi din ke mauqa par Wazeer e Azam  house mein munaqidah taqreeb se khitaab karte hue Nawaz  shareef ne kaha ke malik ko polio se pak karne ke liye jame aagahi hikmat e amli waza ki gayi hai
unhon ne kaha ke hukoomat polio ke khatmay ke liye tamam zaroori iqdamaat kar rahi hai aur jald hi Pakistan  polio se azad malik ban jaye ga
bayan ke mutabiq Wazeer e Azam  neh kaha ke is hkmtِ amli ke tehat polio ke qatray piinaa har bachay ka haq qarar diya gaya hai aur muashray ke par tabqay ke liye zurori hai ke woh bachon ko un ka yeh haq den
Nawaz  shareef ne walidain se appeal ki ke woh polio ke marz ke khatmay keliye hakoomati koshisho ke hissa banin aur –apne bachon ko polio vaccine zaroor pilain
Pakistan  ke sarkari TV ke mutabiq Wazeer e Azam  ney polio day ke mauqa par –apne pegham mein yeh umeed bhi zahir ki hai ke hakoomati koshisho ke nateejay mein polio muhim ke tain awam ke ravayye mein tabdeeli aaye gi aur yeh muhim ziyada kargar saabit hogi
Pakistan  mein polio ke mareezon ki tadaad mein izafay ki wajah walidain ki janib se qatray plwane se inkaar aur polio ke khilaaf chalaye jaanay wali muhim ke amlay par barhatay hue hamlon ko qarar diya jata hai
decemeber دوہزاربارہ se ab taq polio muhim mein shareek health workers aur un ki hifazat par mamoor police ehalkaron par hamlon mein samait saath se ziyada afraad halaak ho chuke hain
sunah دوہزارچودہ ke aaghaz par aqwam mutahidda ke idaara baraye sehat nay﻿ polio ke marz ke phelao ki wajah se Pakistanio  par beron malik safar ke hawalay se pabandiyan aed ki theen
un pabandion ke tehat Pakistan  se beron malik jaaney walon ko rawaangi par yeh certificate faraham karna hota hai ke unhon naay polio vaccine pi hai
polio ka marz ab sirf duniya ke teen mumalik mein paaya jata hai jin mein Pakistan  ke ilawa naijeria aur Afghanistan  shaamil hain
aqwam mutahidda ke bachon ke idaray unicef ke mutabiq jahan Pakistan  mein sunah دوہزارچودہ mein polio ke record mareez samnay aaye hain wahein naijeria aur Afghanistan  mein is marz ke phelao mein kami dekhi gayi hai
idaray ka kehna hai ke jahan is baras Pakistan  mein ab tak polio ke دوسوچھ mareez samnay aa chuke hain wahein naijeria mein is baras sirf chay bachon mein polio ki تشخیص hui jabkay guzashta saal aisay mareezon ki tadaad unchaas thi
Unicef  ke mutabiq aِsi terhan Afghanistan  mein bhi polio ke virus ka phelao intahi kam sun-hwa hai
aqwam mutahidda ke mutabiq, polio se mutasirah teen mumalik duniya bhar ke bachon ke liye khatrah hain aur shaam somalia Iraq  Cameron  aur sati gِni mein mojood virus ki jarrain Pakistan  aur naijeria se mili hain
